<user_name>James Holden<//user_name>< review>
The food was good and came for a great price. The staff is super friendly, not just with me, but with every customer I saw come in. It's a great, friendly environment. The location is in a convenient shopping center, and most people took their food to go (or had it delivered), so there was plenty of seating, indoors and out, that I wouldn't be worried about finding a table. The toppings choices were plentiful, more than certain pizza shops, and they were tasty. We only ordered pizza, but there was tons of other stuff available on the menu as well.<//review>

< text>
Great place for the American style pies many people  grew up with before the pizzas became personal (smaller, thinner and gourmet). Don't get me wrong, the pizzas are good but it won't impress those looking for 'atmosphere'... and really... that is what makes this place super special to me.  This is a pie to take home and share with your friends or family while watching a cool movie on Netflix! Don't miss this little gem tucked in near the Blithedale Whole Foods when you want to chow down on a real AMERICAN pizza.<//text>

<text>Mike's Garlic bread bun was a welcome surprise that hit me the minute the bag came through the window.

The 831 is a must. When I pulled it out, I first mused about why they didn't just wrap the dog in the bacon, but then I bit into it and learned why. Because the hotdog is the star. It had that incredible snap to it, and the Weiner itself was flavorful and juicy in a way that was balanced with saltiness and natural smokieness. The sauce was amazing as well.

If you don't like a complicated dog, I can not emphasis enough how much their hotdog shined as a simple ketchup, mustard, and onion hot dog. The garlic bun on the 831 by comparison is the taste equivalent of almost timid like in relation to the incredible balance of other flavors in this sandwich.  A Gem in our valley.</text>< Pictures>
